

# Pod Autoscaling with Custom Metrics


Creating test namespace "pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111"


## Deploy vLLM with GPU and HPA


Applying vLLM workload with Service, PodMonitor, and HPA


Applying manifest "testdata/pod-autoscaling-workload.yaml" to namespace "pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111"
```bash
> kubectl apply -n pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111 -f testdata/pod-autoscaling-workload.yaml

```

```

resourceclaimtemplate.resource.k8s.io/vllm-qwen25-500m-gpu created
deployment.apps/vllm-qwen25-500m created
service/vllm-qwen25-500m created
podmonitor.monitoring.coreos.com/vllm-qwen25-500m created
horizontalpodautoscaler.autoscaling/vllm-qwen25-500m created

```



Waiting for Deployment vllm-qwen25-500m to be ready
```bash
> kubectl wait -n pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111 --for=condition=Available deployment.apps/vllm-qwen25-500m --timeout=600s

```

```

deployment.apps/vllm-qwen25-500m condition met

```



### Verify vLLM is serving
```bash
> kubectl run vllm-health-check -n pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111 --image=registry.k8s.io/e2e-test-images/agnhost:2.39 --restart=Never --command -- curl -sS http://vllm-qwen25-500m.pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111.svc.cluster.local/health

```

```

pod/vllm-health-check created

```

```bash
> kubectl wait -n pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111 pod/vllm-health-check --for=jsonpath='{.status.phase}'=Succeeded --timeout=120s

```

```

pod/vllm-health-check condition met

```

```bash
> kubectl logs -n pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111 vllm-health-check

```

```


```



vLLM health check response: 


### Verify vLLM exposes Prometheus metrics
```bash
> kubectl run vllm-metrics-check -n pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111 --image=registry.k8s.io/e2e-test-images/agnhost:2.39 --restart=Never --command -- curl -sS http://vllm-qwen25-500m.pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111.svc.cluster.local/metrics

```

```

pod/vllm-metrics-check created

```

```bash
> kubectl wait -n pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111 pod/vllm-metrics-check --for=jsonpath='{.status.phase}'=Succeeded --timeout=120s

```

```

pod/vllm-metrics-check condition met

```

```bash
> kubectl logs -n pod-autoscaling-custom-metric-1774011111 vllm-metrics-check

```
